ti zhi shi kan zuo ren men jing guan de dui xiang ba zhu ke ti zhi jian de guan xi zhi shi kan zuo fan ying he bei fan ying de guan xi er bu shi gai zao he bei gai zao de guan xi suo yi ren shi jiu zhi neng shi xiao ji zhi guan de fan ying er shi bu le jie ren shi de bian zheng ben xing li kai bian zheng fa lai kao cha ren shi wen ti yin er ba fu za de ren shi guo cheng jian dan hua le ba huo sheng sheng de ren shi yun dong ning gu hua le ba duo fang mian de ren shi yao su pian mian hua le zui gen ben de shi ta kan bu dao zhu guan he ke guan zhi jian de mao dun ji qi xiang hu zuo yong mei you ba ren shi kan zuo yi ge bu duan fa zhan de guo cheng ren wei ren shi shi yi ci xing wan cheng de zhe zhong zhi guan de xiao ji bei dong de fan ying lun shi bu ke xue de di san bian zheng wei wu ren shi shi zhu ti dui ke ti de fan ying tong shi you ke fu qi li kai shi jian li kai bian zheng fa kao cha ren shi wen ti de que xian jian chi yi ke xue de she hui shi jian wei te zheng de shi jian wei wu zhu yi ren shi lun ba shi jian de guan dian zuo wei zheng ge ren shi lun de ji chu yi shi jian de guan dian chan shu ren de ren shi huo dong ji qi gui lv ke xue di gui ding le ren shi de zhu ti tong jiu wei wu zhu yi ren shi lun wan quan bu tong de ke xue jie shi er shi ba bian zheng fa ying yong yu fan ying lun kao cha ren shi de fa zhan guo cheng ta ke xue di jie shi le ren shi guo cheng zhong duo fang mian de bian zheng guan xi li ru zhu guan he ke guan ren shi he shi jian gan xing he li xing zhen li de jue dui xing he xiang dui xing zhen li he jia zhi deng fang mian de guan xi ba ren shi kan cheng yi ge you bu zhi dao zhi you qian ru shen de chong man mao dun de neng dong de ren shi guo cheng quan mian di jie shi le ren shi guo cheng de bian zheng xing zhi zhe zhong yi shi jian guan dian he bian zheng guan dian wei te zheng de neng dong fan ying lun bu jin ke fu le jiu wei wu zhu yi ren shi lun de ju xian xing ye che di bo dao le bu ke zhi lun suo ren wei de ren de ren shi neng fou zheng que fan ying ke guan shi wu shi wu fa zheng ming de zhe yi guan dian bian zheng wei wu zhu yi ren shi lun ren wei ren shi de ben zhi shi zhu ti zai shi jian ji chu shang dui ke ti de neng dong fan ying zhe zhong neng dong fan ying bu dan ju you fan ying ke ti nei rong de fan ying xing te zheng er qie ju you shi jian suo yao qiu de zhu ti neng dong de chuang zao xing de te zheng yi fang mian ren shi de fan ying te xing shi ren lei ren shi de ji ben gui ding xing ren shi de fan ying te xing shi zhi ren de ren shi bi ran yao yi ke guan shi wu wei yuan xing he mo ben zai si wei yi fan ying de mo xie xing biao ming le fan ying de ke guan xing ling yi fang mian ren shi de neng dong fan ying ju you chuang zao xing ren shi shi yi zhong zai si wei zhong de neng dong de chuang zao ji shi da dao hen gao de shui ping ye hui you cha bie yin ci zi you shi xiang dui de bu shi jue dui de sui zhao shi jian de shen ru zi you hui bu duan kuo da mao ze dong zhi chu ren lei de li shi jiu shi yi ge bu duan di cong bi ran wang guo xiang zi you wang guo fa zhan de li shi zhe ge li shi yong yuan bu hui wan jie ren lei zong de bu duan di zong jie jing yan you suo fa xian you suo fa ming you suo chuang zao you suo qian jin bi ran yu zi you de guan xi guan chuan yu ren lei cun zai he fa zhan de shi zhong bing cheng wei ren lei cun zai he fa zhan de yong heng mao dun yin ci ye shi ren lei cun zai he fa zhan de yong heng dong li ren lei zai bu duan zhui qiu zi you zhong wan shan zi ji ye zai bu duan jie jue bi ran yu zi you de mao dun guo cheng zhong shi xian fa zhan jian she zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi shi yi ge cong bi ran xiang zi you bu duan qian jin de guo cheng jing guo gai ge kai fang he xian dai hua jian she de bu xie tan suo he jing yan ji lei wo men dang zhu bu shen hua le dui zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi jian she yu fa zhan gui lv de ren shi bing zi jue yun yong gui lv tui jin zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi shi ye wo men jiang geng you neng li tuo shan jie jue feng jian de min zhu yun dong he min zu jie fang yun dong ying xiang ri yi kuo da di yi guo ji cu jin le ma ke si zhu yi de chuan bo he yu guo ji gong ren yun dong de jie he chu bu que li le ma ke si cong gen ben shang xiao chu zi ben zhu yi dao zhi de liang ji fen hua he bu gong ping bu gong zheng xian xiang wei ren de fa zhan ti gong ke kao de bao zhang zhe shi wo men dui she hui zhu yi bao chi bi sheng xin nian de jian shi gen ju ying gai kan dao she hui zhu yi bu jin zai di chao zhong jian chi le xia lai er qie bu duan ji ju li liang shi xian xin de fa zhan xian zai qing kuang yi jing you le xin de bian hua shi jie she hui zhu yi yun dong yi jing kai shi fu su bing chu xian qu yu xing qiang jing fa zhan te bie shi zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi cheng wei shi jie she hui zhu yi yun dong de zhu yao tui dong li liang qi ci chong fen gu ji zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi de cheng gong shi jian dui shi jie she hui zhu yi fa zhan de yi yi jing guo ji shi nian de shi jian tan suo zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi qu de le ju shi zhu mu de hui huang cheng jiu zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi jin ru xin shi dai shi she hui zhu yi shi jian tan suo de xin jing jie zai she hui zhu yi fa zhan shi shang ju you zhong yao di wei bu jin dui zhong guo de she hui zhu yi shi ye ju you zhong da xian shi yi yi er qie dui shi jie she hui zhu yi de fa zhan ju you guang fan ying xiang yao shen ke ren shi dao zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi sui ran zhi shi shi jie she hui zhu yi de yi ge fang mian jun dan zhe shi she hui zhu yi zai yi ge yong you duo nian wen ming shi he yi duo ren kou de dong fang da guo suo qu de de cheng gong shi dang jin shi jie zui da de she hui zhu yi guo jia suo qu de de cheng gong dang jin zhong guo zheng ri yi zou jin shi jie wu tai zhong yang guo ji ying xiang li bu duan ti sheng zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi de li shi xing cheng jiu bi jiang dui shi jie she hui zhu yi de fa zhan tai shi chan sheng zhong da ying xiang ke yi shuo zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi de cheng gong te bie shi zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi jin ru xin shi dai shi shi jie ren min kan dao le she hui zhu yi de qiang da huo li ji da di gu wu le ren men dui she hui zhu yi de xin xin zui hou jian ding xin xin zhen fen jing shen yi kai tuo fen jin de zi tai zou xiang she hui zhu yi guang ming wei lai zhan wang wei lai she hui zhu yi de qian jin dao lu shang huan hui you kun nan he tiao zhan dan zhi yao gong chan dang ren he ren min qun zhong jian ding she hui zhu yi xin nian yong yu zai shi jian zhong kai tuo qian jin shi jie she hui zhu yi jiu yi ding neng zai bu yuan de jiang lai zou xiang fu xing she hui zhu yi wu bai nian de li shi jin cheng yi jing xiong bian di zheng ming ren he li liang du zu dang bu le she hui zhu yi qian jin de bu fa she hui zhu yi zai zhong guo zou guo le xiong guan man dao zhen ru tie de zuo tian zou dao le ren jian zheng dao shi cang sang de jin tian zheng zai zou xiang chang feng po lang hui you shi de mei hao ming tian dang qian zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi jin ru xin shi dai zhong guo ren min zheng zai zhong guo gong chan dang de ling dao xia yi zi xin dan dang de jing shen zhuang tai yi kai tuo fen jin de fen dou zi tai qu kai pi she hui zhu yi de wei lai wo men shen xin zhi yao you feng shan kai lu yu he jia qiao de jing shen you rui yi jin qu da dan tan suo de shi jian jiu yi ding neng ba fu he she hui fa zhan gui lv de she hui zhu yi shi ye bu duan tui xiang qian jin zou xiang she hui zhu yi de guang ming wei lai di qi zhang gong chan zhu yi chong gao li xiang ji qi zui zhong shi xian jiao xue mu de he yao qiu xue xi he zhang wo yu jian wei lai she hui de ke xue fang fa lun yuan ze ba wo gong chan zhu yi she hui de ji ben te zheng shen ke ren shi shi xian gong chan zhu yi de li shi bi ran xing he chang qi xing ba wo gong chan zhu yi yuan da li xiang yu zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi gong tong li xiang de bian zheng guan xi jian ding li xiang xin nian ji ji tou shen xin shi dai zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi shi ye jiao xue yao dian yu jian wei lai she hui de ke xue fang fa lun yuan ze gong chan zhu yi she hui de ji ben te zheng gong chan zhu yi li xiang shi xian de bi ran xing gong chan zhu yi li xiang shi xian de chang qi xing gong chan zhu yi yuan da li xiang yu zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi gong tong li xiang de guan xi she hui zhu yi jing guo chang qi de fa zhan zai gao du fa da de ji chu shang zui zhong jiang zou xiang gong chan zhu yi gong chan zhu yi bu jin shi yi zhong ke xue de li lun he zhe zhong li lun zhi dao xia de xian shi de yun dong er qie shi yi zhong wei lai de she hui zhi du he she hui xing tai shi xian gong chan zhu yi shi ren lei li shi fa zhan de bi ran qu shi shi ma ke si zhu yi zui chong gao de she hui li xiang dang dai da xue sheng ying gai ba wo li shi fa zhan de gui lv shu li zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi gong tong li xiang he gong chan zhu yi yuan da li xiang cong zi wo zuo qi cong xian zai zuo qi zai zhui qiu chong gao li xiang de guo cheng zhong shi xian zi ji de ren sheng jia zhi di yi jie zhan wang wei lai gong chan zhu yi xin she hui yi yu jian wei lai she hui de fang fa lun yuan ze zai zhan wang wei lai she hui de wen ti shang shi fou jian chi ke xue de li chang guan dian fang fa shi neng fou zheng que yu jian wei lai de ji ben qian ti ye shi ma ke si zhu yi yu kong xiang she hui zhu yi de gen ben qu bie ma ke si zhu yi jing dian zuo jia zhan zai ke xue de li chang shang ti chu bing zi jue yun yong le yu jian wei lai she hui de fang fa lun yuan ze zhe shi wo men zhan wang wei lai li xiang she hui de ji ben yi ju tong shi wo men ye ying jie he she hui zhu yi guo jia te bie shi zhong guo fa zhan de li shi jing yan zi jue di yun yong he fa zhan zhe xie ke xue de fang fa lun yuan ze yi zai jie shi ren lei she hui fa zhan yi ban gui lv de ji chu shang zhi ming she hui fa zhan de fang xiang zai ren lei li shi shang you xu xu duo duo si xiang jia re qie di guan zhu zhao ren lei she hui de wei lai bing ti chu zi ji de yu jian te bie shi yi xie kong xiang she hui zhu yi zhe ceng xiang jin di miao hui guo li xiang she hui de tu jing dan zai ma ke si zhu yi chan sheng yi qian ren men dui wei lai she hui de yu jian wang wang dai you nong hou de kong xiang xing zhi he huan xiang se cai yin wei ta men huan mei you zhang wo yu jian wei lai de ke xue fang fa ye bu dong de ren lei she hui fa zhan de ke guan gui lv ma ke si en ge si zhan zai wu chan jie ji li chang shang yun yong ke xue de fang fa zhi li yu yan jiu ren lei she hui te bie shi zi ben zhu yi she hui di yi ci jie shi le she hui fa zhan de yi ban gui lv he zi ben zhu yi she hui fa zhan de te shu gui lv cong er dui gong chan zhu yi she hui zuo chu le ke xue de zhan wang ren lei she hui de fa zhan xiang zi ran jie de fa zhan yi yang ju you zi ji de ke guan gui lv ke xue jie shi zhe xie gui lv jiu neng wei zheng que di li jie guo qu ba wo xian zai he zhan wang wei lai ti gong xiang dao zheng ru lie ning suo zhi chu de ma ke si de quan bu li lun jiu shi yun yong beng kui he wei lai gong chan zhu yi de wei lai de fa zhan er zai pou xi zi ben zhu yi jiu shi jie de guo cheng zhong chan fa wei lai xin shi jie de te dian ma ke si en ge si guan yu wei lai she hui de shi quan ren lei jie fang de gong xing shi mian xiang quan ren lei de zhong guo ren min dang ran yao shu li yuan da li xiang dan zhe ge li xiang bu zhi shu yu zhong guo ren min er shi shu yu quan ren lei yin ci cong zhe ge yi yi shang jiang gong chan zhu yi li xiang ye shi gong tong li xiang er qie shi mian xiang quan ren lei de geng da de gong tong li xiang er zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi gong tong li xiang zhu yao shi mian xiang zhong guo ren min he zhong hua min zu cheng yuan de shi quan ti zhong hua er nv he zhong guo ren min de gong tong li xiang wu yi ju you gong tong xing dan yu quan ren lei xiang bi you ti xian le zhong guo te se ti xian le zhong guo ren min zai she hui zhu yi he gong chan zhu yi li xiang fang mian de ge xing te se dang wo men jiang yao jian ding zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi gong tong li xiang de shi hou bu jin shi zhi zhong guo ren min dui she hui zhu yi li xiang de xiang wang he zhui qiu er qie ye bao han zhao dui zhong guo dao lu de ren tong ji wo men shi tong guo zhong guo zi ji de dao lu lai zhui qiu she hui zhu yi li xiang he gong chan zhu yi yuan da li xiang zhe zhong zhong guo te se he min zu te se bing mei you fou ding li xiang de gong tong yuan ze er shi ba gong tong yuan ze yu guo qing min qing xiang jie he shi she hui zhu yi he gong chan zhu yi li xiang zhan xian chu geng feng fu de se cai zong zhi bi xu yi bian zheng si wei ba wo he chu li yuan da li xiang he gong tong li xiang de guan xi bu neng yong jian dan hua de tai du lai dui dai ta er shi yao yong ma ke si zhu yi de bian zheng si wei he li shi si wei qu ba wo ta ren he shi hou du yao jian chi yuan da li xiang he gong tong li xiang de tong yi bu neng ba ta men ge lie kai lai dui li qi lai mei you yuan da li xiang de zhi yin jiu bu hui you gong tong li xiang de que li he jian chi mei you gong tong li xiang de shi xian yuan da li xiang jiu mei you xian shi de ji chu wang ji yuan da li xiang er zhi gu yan qian jiu hui shi qu qian jin de fang xiang li kai xian shi gong zuo er kong tan yuan da li xiang jiu hui tuo li shi ji zhe shi wo men dang zai chang qi shi jian zhong de chu de ji ben jie lun er jian ding li xiang xin nian tou shen xin shi dai zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi shi ye xi jin ping zhi chu qing nian shi biao zhi shi dai de zui ling min de qing yu biao shi dai de ze ren fu yu qing nian shi dai de guang rong shu yu qing nian qing nian shi zu guo de wei lai min zu de xi wang qing nian xing ze guo jia xing qing nian qiang ze guo jia qiang shi xian zhong hua min zu wei da fu xing de zhong guo meng duo qu xin shi dai zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi de wei da sheng li jiang quan guo ge zu ren min de gong tong li xiang bian wei xian shi xu yao yi dai you yi dai you zhi qing nian jie xu fen dou qing nian yi dai de li xiang xin nian jing shen zhuang tai zong he su zhi shi yi ge guo jia fa zhan huo li de zhong yao ti xian ye shi yi ge guo jia he xin jing zheng li de zhong yao yin su qing nian yi dai you li xiang you ben ling you dan dang guo jia jiu you qian tu min zu jiu you xi wang yi dai qing nian you yi dai qing nian de li shi ji yu dang qian zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi jin ru xin shi dai zhe ge xin shi dai shi cheng qian qi hou ji wang kai lai zai xin de li shi tiao jian xia ji xu duo qu zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi wei da sheng li de shi dai shi jue sheng quan mian jian cheng xiao kang she hui jin er quan mian jian she she hui zhu yi xian dai hua qiang guo de shi dai shi quan guo ge zu ren min tuan jie fen dou bu duan chuang zao mei hao sheng huo zhu bu shi xian quan ti ren min gong tong fu yu de shi dai shi quan ti zhong hua er nv lu li tong xin fen li shi xian zhong hua min zu wei da fu xing zhong guo meng de shi dai shi wo guo ri yi zou jin shi jie wu tai zhong yang bu duan wei ren lei zuo chu geng da gong xian de shi dai zhe yi zhan xin de shi dai wei dang dai qing nian te bie shi dang dai da xue sheng ti gong le shi shi ren sheng cai hua de ji wei you li de li shi ji yu xin shi dai de qing nian bi xu jian ding li xiang xin nian xi jin ping zhi chu qing nian shi dai shu li zheng que de li xiang jian ding de xin nian shi fen jin yao bu jin yao shu li er qie yao zai xin zhong zha gen yi bei zi du neng jian chi wei zhi fen dou li xiang xin nian shi jing shen shang de gai shi ren de jing shen zhi zhu he jing shen ji liang shi gu wu ren men qian jin he fen dou de qiang da jing shen dong li li xiang xin nian dong yao shi zui wei xian de dong yao li xiang xin nian hua po shi zui wei xian de hua po xin zhong you xin yang jiao xia cai hui you li liang dang dai da xue sheng yao jian ding li xiang xin nian zi jue zuo zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi gong tong li xiang de jian ding xin yang zhe zhong cheng shi jian zhe wei ci jiu yao shen ru xue xi ma ke si zhu yi ji ben yuan li ji ma ke si zhu yi zhong guo hua de li lun cheng guo te bie shi xue xi xi jin ping xin shi dai zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi si xiang rang zhen li wu zhuang wo men de tou nao rang zhen li zhi yin wo men de li xiang rang zhen li jian ding wo men de xin yang yao jian chi xue er xin xue er yong xue er xing ba xue xi cheng guo zhuan hua wei bu ke han dong de li xiang xin nian zhuan hua wei zheng que de shi jie guan ren sheng guan jia zhi guan yong li xiang zhi guang zhao liang fen dou zhi lu yong xin yang zhi li kai chuang mei hao wei lai dang dai qing nian yao ji ji tou shen xin shi dai zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi shi ye yong zuo dan dang zhong hua min zu wei da fu xing da ren de shi dai xin ren wo men de guo jia zheng zai zou xiang fan rong fu qiang wo men de min zu zheng zai zou xiang wei da fu xing wo men de ren min zheng zai zou xiang geng jia xing fu mei hao de sheng huo zhan wang wei lai wo guo qing nian yi dai jian fu li shi zhong ren bi jiang da you ke wei ye bi jiang da you zuo wei dang dai zhong guo qing nian yao tou shen xin shi dai zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi shi ye tou shen dang he ren min zai zhong guo te se she hui zhu yi xin shi dai de wei da fen dou yao yi yong yu dan dang de jing shen zuo zou zai xin shi dai qian lie de fen jin zhe kai tuo zhe feng xian zhe yi zhi zhao de xin nian you liang de pin de feng fu de zhi shi guo ying de ben ling tong ren min qun zhong
